if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') != 'd269e854d3361d9ffbfd74376d0e4f67d538f703') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== 'd269e854d3361d9ffbfd74376d0e4f67d538f703') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== 'd038490f5ab6082d4a5b7a72f33e07d9a989fd7e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt') !== 'd269e854d3361d9ffbfd74376d0e4f67d538f703') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/developer_notes/feature_oids.txt');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.css.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') != '01e9d12ed39f73f191105903e7ec67952b7a8eb0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.css.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.css.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '01e9d12ed39f73f191105903e7ec67952b7a8eb0') {

			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.css.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.css.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.css.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.css.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '01e9d12ed39f73f191105903e7ec67952b7a8eb0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');

	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd') != '8dcf46623a0313f9b516c1b6260ccf4c7476dad1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd') !== '8dcf46623a0313f9b516c1b6260ccf4c7476dad1') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd') !== 'fdfc503b82ad98dac510bf9058d157b31b6ad0cd') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd') !== '8dcf46623a0313f9b516c1b6260ccf4c7476dad1') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/manifest_plugin_page.xsd');
		}
	}
}
